black solid;padding-top: 15px;\">Inflation Calculators</h1>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>We've assembled a variety of \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinflation calculators to suit your every need \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\twhether you want to calculate inflation by specific \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tmonth or just by year. We even have developed a fun \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"steam punk\" inflation calculator that goes back to \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t1774 and even estimates future inflation. </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>Of course we also provide the official&nbsp; U.S. \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tBureau of Labor Statistics Inflation calculator as \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\twell.&nbsp; Plus a U.K. Inflation calculator (price \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconverter based on year). </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>We have also updated our Cumulative Inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCalculator which calculates inflation down to \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tspecific months giving it a cool new look and the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tability to not only provide the cumulative inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\trate but also show changes in purchasing power.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()--></div>\n\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t<div class=\"home-middle\">\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"home-middle-left widget-area\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-4\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%201%20top\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do not remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h2 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">Steampunk Inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCalculator</h2>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<iframe id=\"spcalc\" name=\"IframeCalc\" scrolling=\"no\" src=\"calc/steampunk-inflation-calculator.html\" style=\"width: 325px; height: 533px; border: 0;\" title=\"Steampunk Inflation Calculator\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tYour browser does not support inline frames or is currently \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconfigured not to display inline frames. \t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</iframe>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"auto-style6\"><strong>Hit Enter to Calculate</strong> <br>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t(Be Patient remember \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthis is Steampunk Technology <br>it takes a \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tmoment to build up steam! )</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"auto-style2\" style=\"padding: 10px;\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tThe steampunk inflation calculator was designed \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tto be a fun way to calculate U.S. inflation from \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t1774 through future estimates up to 2024. So it \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tis not only a past inflation calculator but also \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\ta <strong><em>\"future inflation calculator\" </em>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</strong>as well.<strong><em>&nbsp; </em>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</strong>It calculates \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthe inflation rate and inflation adjusted prices \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tusing conversion factors created by\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"http://oregonstate.edu/cla/polisci/download-conversion-factors\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tOregon State University economists</a>. <br>For \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthe period from 1913 - present, the data is \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbased on the annual average U.S. Bureau of Labor \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tStatistics CPI so it will produce the same \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tresult as the BLS Inflation Calculator (see \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbelow) but it also combines other data sources \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tfor the periods outside the range available from \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthe BLS. The Steam Punk Inflation Calculator tells you the cumulative \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinflation rate over the period chosen \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<span class=\"auto-style5\">plus</span>&nbsp;the inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tadjusted price of a starting value of your choice.<br>Simply enter the starting year, ending year and \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tstarting value and hit your enter key. <br>Remember this is a \"SteamPunk\" calculator so it \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\ttakes a moment to build up enough steam to \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tgenerate an answer. Please be patient and enjoy \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\twatching the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tlights flash and the gears spin. <br>You can click the \"reset\" button \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tto try different numbers and watch the fun again.<br>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tA special thanks to Dana Mattocks for creating the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tamazing \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\toriginal SteamPunk Computer that this calculator \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\twas based upon and his generous\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://www.flickr.com/photos/steampunkfrankenstein/3340799972/in/photostream/\" rel=\"nofollow\" target=\"_blank\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcreative commons license of the original photo</a>.\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_end --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-6\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%201%20middle%20top\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do no remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">BLS Inflation Calculator</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page type-page status-publish entry gfwa-1 gfwa-odd\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p class=\"auto-style6\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Calculators/Inflation_Calculator.asp\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt=\"US Bureau of Labor Statistics Inflation calculator\" src=\"Inflation/images/BLSInflationCalculator.jpg\" style=\"height: 231px\" width=\"280\"></a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>The official&nbsp; \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Calculators/Inflation_Calculator.asp\">U.S. Bureau of Labor Statistics \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tInflation calculator</a> is based on the CPI data \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthey calculate every month. It is a quick and \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\teasy way to calculate basic changes in \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpurchasing power using average data by year but \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdoes not provide the cumulative inflation rate \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tbetween two points or the accuracy down to a \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tspecific month.&nbsp;For greater accuracy or \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcumulative inflation use our\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Calculators/Cumulative_Inflation_Calculator.aspx\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCumulative Inflation Calculator</a>.&nbsp;<a class=\"more-link\" href=\"https://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Calculators/Inflation_Calculator.asp\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t[Read More...]</a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_end --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-6\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%201%20middle\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do no remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">Inflation Adjusted \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tElectricity Prices</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page type-page status-publish entry gfwa-1 gfwa-odd\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt=\"Inflation Adjusted Electricity Prices\" class=\"alignnone\" height=\"180\" src=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/wp-content/uploads/2012/07/Inflation-Adjusted-Electricity-348x180.jpg\" width=\"348\"><p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tElectricity Price Inflation Residential electricity \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tprices in the U.S. have risen from an average of \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t7.83 cents per kilowatthour in 1990 to an average \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tof 11.44 cents per kwh in 2010. This is a 46% increase \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tin 20 years and sounds like a lot but as …\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a class=\"more-link\" href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/inflation-adjusted-prices/electricity-price-inflation-rate/\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t[Read More...]</a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_end --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-8\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%201%20middle%20bottom\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do no remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">Misery Index</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page type-page status-publish entry gfwa-1 gfwa-odd\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a class=\"alignnone\" href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/misery-index/\" title=\"Misery Index\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt=\"US Misery Index August 2013\" class=\"alignnone\" height=\"180\" src=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/wp-content/uploads/2013/08/US_Misery_Index_Aug_2013-348x180.jpg\" width=\"348\"></a><p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tThe original misery index was not created by Robert \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tBarro as some people mistakenly believe. He created \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthe “Barro Misery Index” (BMI) in 1999, which also \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tincludes interest rates and GDP trend into the mix. \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tThe standard original Misery index was …\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a class=\"more-link\" href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/misery-index/\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t[Read More...]</a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_end --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-10\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%201%20bottom\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do no remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">Inflation Definitions</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li><a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2010/07/21/real-definition-inflation/\" title=\"Inflation Definition\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tInflation</a> is often defined as \"an increase in the price you pay for goods\" or a \"decline in the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tpurchasing power of your money\".<br>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li><li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2008/07/16/inflation-cause-and-effect/\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tInflation causes</a>  - price inflation is often \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcaused by an increase in the money supply thus \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdecreasing the actual value of each individual unit \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tof currency.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2008/02/24/what-is-core-inflation-and-why-doesnt-it-include-food-and-energy/\" title=\"What is Core Inflation?\">Core Inflation</a> \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tis used primarily by academics to calculate the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tunderlying inflation rate based on an increase \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tin the money supply and is not terribly relevant \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tto the average consumer because it doesn't \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinclude the volatile food and energy components. \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tThe opposite of core inflation is the\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"<a href=\"inflationdata.com/articles/2014/07/10/poverty-matters-capitalists/#walmart\">Walmart Inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tIndex</a>\" designed by Charles \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tGave to include only Rent, Energy and Food since \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthat is what the \"working poor\" who frequently \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tshop at Walmart spend most of their income on.\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2008/07/16/what-is-deflation/\" title=\"Deflation\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tDeflation </a> is generally considered to be \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\"falling prices\". But it has a variety of causes and \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcan be either good or bad for an economy depending \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\ton its cause.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2008/11/19/disinflation-what-is-it/\" title=\"Disinflation\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tDisinflation</a><a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2008/11/19/disinflation-what-is-it/\"><span class=\"auto-style3\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</span></a>is a slowing or decrease in the rate of \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinflation. It is not to be confused with deflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\twhich is actual falling prices. In disinflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tprices are still rising simply not as fast as they \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tonce were.\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tThe term\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2011/02/16/agflation-what-is-it/\" title=\"Agflation\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tAgflation</a> was coined in 2007 by Merrill Lynch \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tanalysts to describe the economic condition at the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\ttime whereby rising demand for agricultural products \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\twas driving up overall prices. The primary driver of \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tagricultural prices was legislation requiring \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tethanol use in gasoline, thus increasing demand for \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcorn.</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tThe term\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2008/11/19/stagflation-what-is-it/\" title=\"Stagflation\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tStagflation</a> was coined during the 1970's \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tto describe the inflationary but stagnant economic \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tconditions. </li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/hyperinflation/\" title=\"Hyperinflation\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tHyperinflation</a><a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/hyperinflation/\"><span class=\"auto-style3\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</span></a>is typically associated with\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2010/09/20/hyperinflation-in-weimar-germany/\" title=\"Weimar Germany\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tWeimar Germany </a>but other well-known cases \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinclude\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/confederate-inflation/\" title=\"Confederate Inflation Rates (1861 – 1865)\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tConfederate Civil War Inflation </a>and\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/2008/07/16/zimbabwean-hyperinflation-officially-estimated-at-2-2-million-percent/\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tZimbabwean Hyperinflation</a>. Although there is no \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tabsolute pecentage where ordinary inflation turns \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinto \"hyperinflation\" typically hyperinflation gets \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tprogressively worse until the economy implodes.\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</li>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</ul>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_end --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"home-middle-right widget-area\">\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-5\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%202%20top\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do no remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">Cumulative Inflation Calculator</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page type-page status-publish gfwa-1 gfwa-odd\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"Inflation/Inflation_Calculators/Cumulative_Inflation_Calculator.aspx\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<img alt=\"Cumulative Inflation Calculator\" src=\"Inflation/images/iPhoneInflationCalculator-500.jpg\"></a>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tSwitching from the archaic steampunk inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcalculator to the modern \"Smartphone\" design we \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\thave our updated Cumulative Inflation Calculator \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\twhich allows you to calculate inflation by month \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tand year rather than simply using a yearly \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\taverage. The results \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tprovide a total cumulative inflation rate from \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthe start date to the end date and an inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tadjusted price based on the starting value you \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tprovide.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tInflation calculations are based strictly on the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tU.S. Bureau of Labor statistics\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Consumer_Price_Index/CurrentCPI.asp\" title=\"Current CPI Data\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCPI data</a> and are therefore limited to the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdates from 1913 - Present.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a class=\"more-link\" href=\"https://inflationdata.com/Inflation/Inflation_Calculators/Cumulative_Inflation_Calculator.aspx\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t[Try \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthe Cumulative Inflation Calculator Here...]</a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_end --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-7\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%202%20middle%20top\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do no remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">U.K. Inflation \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCalculator (Pounds)</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page type-page status-publish entry gfwa-1 gfwa-odd\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<script src=\"http://safalra.com/other/historical-uk-inflation-price-conversion/widget.js\" type=\"text/javascript\"></script>\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>The U.K. Inflation Calculator works much like \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tthe official BLS inflation calculator in that it \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tonly calculates changes in price based on the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\taverage annual index and doesn't provide a \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tcumulative inflation total. </p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>The U.K. inflation calculator uses the U.K. Retail Prices Index \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tand is capable of calculating inflation all the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tway back to 1751. It calculates a \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tprice comparison between&nbsp; different \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tdates in Pounds, taking into consideration the \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tU.K. inflation rate rather than the U.S. Dollar \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tinflation rate.</p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>So for instance, \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tif something cost £100 in 1900 it would cost £11,000 \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tin 2013. To use the Historical Price Converter​ \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tsimply enter a value and use the pull-down menus \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tto choose a starting and ending date and the converter \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\twill tell you the value on the other date. \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<a href=\"https://inflationdata.com/articles/uk-historical-price-converter/\" title=\"UK Historical Price Converter\"> [Read \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tMore...] </a></p>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t</div>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #EndEditable -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--end post_class()-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_end --></div>\n\t\t\t\t\t</section>\n\t\t\t\t\t<section id=\"featured-post-7\" class=\"widget featuredpost\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"widget-wrap\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- #BeginEditable \"column%202%20middle\" -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!--do no remove classes-->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<h4 class=\"widget-title widgettitle\">Cost of Living \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\tCalculator</h4>\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<!-- google_ad_section_start -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<div class=\"page type-page status-publish entry gfwa-1 gfwa-odd\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\t<p>The cost of maintaining a certain lifestyle varies from state to state \n\t\t\t\t\t\t\t\tand even from city to city within a state.
